    <div class="card">
    <div class="card-header" id="headingADDED_fields_transport">
    <h2 class="mb-0">
    <button aria-controls="ADDED_fields_transport" aria-expanded="" class="btn btn-link property-name-button" data-target="#ADDED_fields_transport" data-toggle="collapse" onclick="setAnchor('#ADDED_fields_transport')" type="button"><span class="property-name">transport</span> <span class="badge badge-warning required-property">Required</span></button>
    </h2>
    </div>
    <div aria-labelledby="headingADDED_fields_transport" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionADDED_fields_transport" id="ADDED_fields_transport">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Transport</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>Method of snapshots transfer.</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SSH</code> transfers snapshots via SSH connection. This method is supported everywhere but does not achieve       great performance.</li>
    <li><code>SSH+NETCAT</code> uses unencrypted connection for data transfer. This can only be used in trusted networks       and requires a port (specified by range from <code>netcat_active_side_port_min</code> to <code>netcat_active_side_port_max</code>)       to be open on <code>netcat_active_side</code>.</li>
    <li><code>LOCAL</code> replicates to or from localhost.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="ADDED_fields_transport_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SSH"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SSH+NETCAT"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"LOCAL"</li></ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>

    <div class="card">
    <div class="card-header" id="headingADDED_fields_readonly">
    <h2 class="mb-0">
    <button aria-controls="ADDED_fields_readonly" aria-expanded="" class="btn btn-link property-name-button" data-target="#ADDED_fields_readonly" data-toggle="collapse" onclick="setAnchor('#ADDED_fields_readonly')" type="button"><span class="property-name">readonly</span></button>
    </h2>
    </div>
    <div aria-labelledby="headingADDED_fields_readonly" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionADDED_fields_readonly" id="ADDED_fields_readonly">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Readonly</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span> <span class="badge badge-success default-value">Default: "SET"</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>Controls destination datasets readonly property.</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SET</code>: Set all destination datasets to readonly=on after finishing the replication.</li>
    <li><code>REQUIRE</code>: Require all existing destination datasets to have readonly=on property.</li>
    <li><code>IGNORE</code>: Avoid this kind of behavior.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="ADDED_fields_readonly_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SET"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"REQUIRE"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"IGNORE"</li></ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>

    <button aria-controls="ADDED_fields_retention_policy" aria-expanded="" class="btn btn-link property-name-button" data-target="#ADDED_fields_retention_policy" data-toggle="collapse" onclick="setAnchor('#ADDED_fields_retention_policy')" type="button"><span class="property-name">retention_policy</span> <span class="badge badge-warning required-property">Required</span></button>
    </h2>
    </div>
    <div aria-labelledby="headingADDED_fields_retention_policy" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionADDED_fields_retention_policy" id="ADDED_fields_retention_policy">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Retention Policy</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>How to delete old snapshots on target side:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SOURCE</code>: Delete snapshots that are absent on source side.</li>
    <li><code>CUSTOM</code>: Delete snapshots that are older than <code>lifetime_value</code> and <code>lifetime_unit</code>.</li>
    <li><code>NONE</code>: Do not delete any snapshots.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="ADDED_fields_retention_policy_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SOURCE"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"CUSTOM"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"NONE"</li></ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>

    <h2 class="mb-0">
    <button aria-controls="CHANGED_fields_transport" aria-expanded="" class="btn btn-link property-name-button" data-target="#CHANGED_fields_transport" data-toggle="collapse" onclick="setAnchor('#CHANGED_fields_transport')" type="button"><span class="property-name">transport</span> <span class="badge badge-warning required-property">Required</span></button>
    </h2>
    </div>
    <div aria-labelledby="headingCHANGED_fields_transport" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionCHANGED_fields_transport" id="CHANGED_fields_transport">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Transport</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>Method of snapshots transfer.</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SSH</code> transfers snapshots via SSH connection. This method is supported everywhere but does not achieve       great performance.</li>
    <li><code>SSH+NETCAT</code> uses unencrypted connection for data transfer. This can only be used in trusted networks       and requires a port (specified by range from <code>netcat_active_side_port_min</code> to <code>netcat_active_side_port_max</code>)       to be open on <code>netcat_active_side</code>.</li>
    <li><code>LOCAL</code> replicates to or from localhost.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="CHANGED_fields_transport_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SSH"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SSH+NETCAT"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"LOCAL"</li></ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>

    <button aria-controls="CHANGED_fields_readonly" aria-expanded="" class="btn btn-link property-name-button" data-target="#CHANGED_fields_readonly" data-toggle="collapse" onclick="setAnchor('#CHANGED_fields_readonly')" type="button"><span class="property-name">readonly</span></button>
    </h2>
    </div>
    <div aria-labelledby="headingCHANGED_fields_readonly" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionCHANGED_fields_readonly" id="CHANGED_fields_readonly">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Readonly</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span> <span class="badge badge-success default-value">Default: "SET"</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>Controls destination datasets readonly property.</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SET</code>: Set all destination datasets to readonly=on after finishing the replication.</li>
    <li><code>REQUIRE</code>: Require all existing destination datasets to have readonly=on property.</li>
    <li><code>IGNORE</code>: Avoid this kind of behavior.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="CHANGED_fields_readonly_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SET"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"REQUIRE"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"IGNORE"</li></ul>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>
    </div>

    <div aria-labelledby="headingCHANGED_fields_retention_policy" class="collapse property-definition-div" data-parent="#accordionCHANGED_fields_retention_policy" id="CHANGED_fields_retention_policy">
    <div class="card-body pl-5">
    <h4>Retention Policy</h4><span class="badge badge-dark value-type">Type: enum (of string)</span><br/>
    <span class="description"><p>How to delete old snapshots on target side:</p>
    <ul>
    <li><code>SOURCE</code>: Delete snapshots that are absent on source side.</li>
    <li><code>CUSTOM</code>: Delete snapshots that are older than <code>lifetime_value</code> and <code>lifetime_unit</code>.</li>
    <li><code>NONE</code>: Do not delete any snapshots.</li>
    </ul>
    </span><div class="enum-value" id="CHANGED_fields_retention_policy_enum">
    <h5>Must be one of:</h5>
    <ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"SOURCE"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"CUSTOM"</li><li class="list-group-item enum-item">"NONE"</li></ul>
    </div>
